## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the fundamental problem in population dynamics. The relationship encodes how population change depends on current population size and potentially time-varying environmental factors.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Malthusian growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (exponential growth/decline, density-independent)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth with logarithmic density dependence)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Strong Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (cooperative growth at low density)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with hyperbolic saturation)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible sigmoidal growth model)
- Time-varying logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal carrying capacity)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P / (P + c3) (logistic with Holling type II harvesting)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic growth model)
- Time-dependent Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponentially changing growth rate)
- Logistic with immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 (logistic growth plus constant immigration)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional-order density dependence)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Quadratic dependence on P (P - P² terms) → logistic-type density regulation with a carrying capacity
- Cubic dependence on P (P² - P³ or P·(P-a)·(1-P/K)) → Allee effect with critical population threshold
- Logarithmic dependence P·log(K/P) → Gompertz-type growth with asymmetric sigmoid trajectory
- Ratio P/(P+c) appearing in loss terms → Holling type II functional response (predation/harvesting saturation)
- Multiplicative separation f(P)·g(t) → environmental modulation of intrinsic population dynamics
- Additive constant term independent of P → immigration/stocking or constant external input
- Sinusoidal time dependence in coefficients → seasonal or periodic environmental forcing
- Growth rate per capita (dP_dt/P) decreasing linearly with P → classic logistic regulation
- Product of two linear factors in P → bistability or two equilibrium points in population dynamics
- Exponential decay in time multiplying growth terms → deteriorating habitat or resource depletion over time
